<Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
A beautiful and perfect place for prayer, reflection, meditation, and contemplation. Everytime I go, I leave feeling more peaceful and more happy. The church is beautiful inside, especially the chapel. The prayer trails are amazing. Last time I walked the prayer trail containing the "Way of the Cross". I prayed all the stations with my friend, and the setting and atmosphere allowed us to really meditate on the stations of the cross. The views are spectacular. The prayer trails serve as a perfect place to enjoy, take in, and appreciate wilderness. The gift shop has an impressive collection of books, art, gifts, accessories, etc. The library is also of a good size and has many books to utilize for prayer and study. The grounds also serves as a center for retreats and spiritual activities and events, so if you're considering having some type of activity or event, I highly suggest the Prince of Peace abbey!<//Review>

< text>
I spent a weekend retreat at the abbey this March, 2013. It has been some time since I went to a retreat at any Catholic facility, probably 50 years. The monks were very approachable, helpful, and had the face of someone in close contact with their savior. There is a great opportunity to join in worship and prayer with them in their church. They took care that I was able to find my place and sing the Psalms with them each day. Their life is dedicated to knowing their savior and it reflects in their souls. Such a welcome relief from this world. The rooms are quiet and very clean. The food is served well and on time. You can walk on the top of their mesa in quietness and reflection looking at the California coastal chaparral. This gave me a chance to retreat with my savior and I enjoyed it.<//text>

<review>We stopped in for our weekly dinner out and this was a good choice. It was suggested while at work this week and what a great suggestion.

The service was good and the food was excellent.

We ordered: Chicken Tikka (dry, not wet), Sag Paneer (medium spicy), and Chana Masala (spicy).

The Chicken tikka was cooked perfectly and it was tender and served still sizzling; SOO good.

The Sag Paneer was super flavorful.

The Chana Masala was out of this world and not too spicy.

Everything was cooked fresh and it showed. We left full, not overly full, and very satisfied. Oh yeah we even got some Barfi for the house; Very fresh.

If you like Indian food give this place a shot you should be pleased.

07/03/2020

< Rating>
4</Rating>
< Review>
Good food for a small local restaurant. Food is a 4/5. Service 4/5. Atmosphere is a generous 3/5 (not someplace I'd take my wife on a date night, would just order as take out.) but is ok as a quick dine-in. Cost is 4/5 (fair), not cheap but definitely not overpriced.

Do NOT take this review as a negative, but a comparison to other restaurants. It is a small "mom-and-pop" style. This is more of a niche establishment that gives the community a valuable unique choice when the age old question "what would you like to eat?" comes up. I should note that I've eaten here over a handful of times since 2019, and return often when I'm in the mood for Indian cuisine (but am too lazy to cook it). As an aside I've been an amateur chef for almost 20 yrs and can duplicate most dishes by taste alone (no recipe needed).

Try them out for yourself. Its definitely worth a taste if you're looking for something different.< /Review>
